<div id="review_1513020077" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1513020077" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1513020077?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781785652486" href="/book/show/40139338-vengeful">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=superheroes">superheroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=thriller-crime">thriller-crime</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1513020077" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6736184375920921964"><b>And that was entirely INTENSE.</b> Also long so I feel like I was just flung down 57 flights of stairs and am now gasping at the end with my leGS brOKEn. Although I will admit I liked Vicious better and I'm a teeny bit disappointed because I expected a 5star read and (for me) it wasn't. But like it was still excellent.<br/><br/>I'm absolutely <i>reeling</i> with the cleverness of the timelines. I understand why Schwab was dying on twitter while writing this. I've written a teeny-tiny 2-timeline split book and that n</span>
  <span id="freeText6736184375920921964" style="display:none"><b>And that was entirely INTENSE.</b> Also long so I feel like I was just flung down 57 flights of stairs and am now gasping at the end with my leGS brOKEn. Although I will admit I liked Vicious better and I'm a teeny bit disappointed because I expected a 5star read and (for me) it wasn't. But like it was still excellent.<br /><br />I'm absolutely <i>reeling</i> with the cleverness of the timelines. I understand why Schwab was dying on twitter while writing this. I've written a teeny-tiny 2-timeline split book and that near killed me. But this has DOZENS AND DOZENS OF THEM. <b>This book is a work of intricate design and it's staggering and very worthy of applause.</b><br /><br /><b>We also get two new characters sweeping the page: Marcella and June.</b> One thing that annoyed me about Vicious was the lack of women so this MORE than makes up for it. They are badass and terrifying. Marcella is wickedly beautiful and so Slytherin afjdksald I absolutely loved her. She just grew into this frightful villain of <i>perfection</i>. (Shhhh I'm allowed to love the villains.) And June is a shape-shifter of many many mysteries. I wish we got some answers for her? But she looks out for Sydney and plays all sides and LOVE HER.<br /><br />Basically this:<br /><blockquote>Schwab: here is a new backstabbing Slytherin character<br />Me: LOVE !! AM IN !! LOVE !!!</blockquote><br />Who is not a Slytherin here, hmm? (Ok Mitch and Sydney are Hufflepuffs, but still.)<br /><br /><b>Eli and Victor actually don't feature as much?</b> Well Victor is dying and trying to find a cure and Eli is in prison but working with Stell. We get Eli's backstory which made me feEL THINGS FOR HIM I DIDN'T ASK TO FEEL. Like rip my heart (literally) out of my chest, thanks. Tbh, I don't see a difference between Eli and Victor. Just that Eli thinks he's good (he's not) and Victor thinks he's bad (he is). They are such a fantastic duo and will literally <i>plan to save each other</i> so <i>THEY</i> can be the one to kill the other. I can't even. Bless them.<br /><br /><b>Also, no joke, my favourite scenes were the domestic ones.</b> My dysfunctional family of Victor, Mitch and Sydney. Afjsdakl. The chapters are like: mURDER MURDER ... hot chocolate and homeschooling Sydney!! I love it. I love that Victor pretends not to care but he loves them.<br /><br /><b>Dislikes?</b> Just that it was long, very very long, and I felt it dragged in the middle. And I missed having Victor feature more. It felt like his character just stagnated? The ending was unsatisfying for me tbh.<br /><br /><b>ALSO IT IS VICIOUSLY STABBY.</b> Which I freaking adore. The powers are <i>intense</i> and creative and we get Mob bosses and government agencies and vivisection and blood everywhere and ajfdskald everyone gets hurt and I love it all. <b>Vicious</b> wins for me, but Vengeful is still a stunning sequel.<br /><br /><blockquote>Her eyes narrowed in concentration as her will warred with his, but Eli was loose, and Sydney was lost, and those two things made Victor immovable.</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="6736184375920921964" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2563573010" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3754124495545817501">i just have one question, <b>what in the hell just happened?</b><br/><br/>that is all<br/><br/>Im simultaneously destroyed and yet so fulfilled and content at this ending<br/><br/>I cant believe this story is over <s>for the time being</s>, I genuinely felt like I was living with them GOSH DAMMIT<br/><br/>-	I cant even begin to describe what this book did to me<br/>-	Victor vale: a madman, book defiler, a soft dad, just wants to feel <b>alive</b> again and honestly relatable<br/>-	Mitch: a marshmallow that got stuck inside a rugby player’s body, the other soft dad,</span>
  <span id="freeText3754124495545817501" style="display:none">i just have one question, <b>what in the hell just happened?</b><br /><br />that is all<br /><br />Im simultaneously destroyed and yet so fulfilled and content at this ending<br /><br />I cant believe this story is over <s>for the time being</s>, I genuinely felt like I was living with them GOSH DAMMIT<br /><br />-	I cant even begin to describe what this book did to me<br />-	Victor vale: a madman, book defiler, a soft dad, just wants to feel <b>alive</b> again and honestly relatable<br />-	Mitch: a marshmallow that got stuck inside a rugby player’s body, the other soft dad, but hes <b>softer</b>, secret genius<br />-	(the hot chocolate and grilled cheese scene!!!!!)<br />-	Sydney: my daughter, perpetually smol, she just wants the best for everyone, love animals, wants friends. Again, relatable <br />-	(THEYRE A FAMILY AAAAAAA)<br />-	Eli: hurt, sad, hurt, alone, hurt. IM TRYING NOT TO SYMPATHIZE BUT GUYS HIS BACKSTORY IS SO SAD <br />-	Marcella: a queen amidst of peasants, will steal your man…..and then kill him, her makeup is always flawless, is always ready to cut a bixch<br />-	June: fav, indecisive about who she should be, loyal…but she comes first, the cool kid you always wanted to be<br />-	THESE CHARACTERS CAME TO LIFE<br />-	I don’t know how schwab was able to do it, but they were all so real and genuine, not a single one was alike, im honestly shocked at how she was able to craft them so well<br />-	I seriously love this book with all my being<br />-	Its action packed, fast paced, has that hint of comedic edge, its so damn genius <br />-	The way the plot comes together and ties back to the beginning <br />-	There is no boring moments, I was honestly gripped from the first sentence till the very end<br />-	The two new characters (Marcella &amp; june) really added a new dimension to the story<br />-	Like yes we love victor and mitch and Sydney and the little messed up family they built but consider this<br />-	Two ladies who aren’t scared of power and are always underestimated and are Tired of it<br />-	Like imagine what they could accomplish!!<br />-	Can I just say the highlight of the story was mitch being domestic<br />-	WHY WERE THERE SO FEW HOT CHOCOLATE SCENES??? <br />-	PETITION TO GET A SHORT STORY WHERE MITCH AND VICTOR TAKE SYDNEY TO A FAIR AND THEY GET COTTON CANDY AND RIDE THE CAROUSEL AND PLAY BUMPER CARS AND VICTOR BROODS THE WHOLE TIME BUT SECRETLY LOVES IT<br />-	Okay im losing focus<br />-	ANYWAYS<br />-	THAT<br />-	ENDING<br />-	LIKE IT WAS SATISFYING BUT IT MADE ME SAD<br />-	And the last 50 pages??? Wild my friends, wild<br />-	Im just a mixture of the crying emoji and heart eyes emoji with a hint of pain emoji and I don’t know how to go on emoji<br />-	In conclusion<br />-	Read the damn book<br />-	<s>hope youre happy, emily 😒 </s><br /><br /><br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br /><br />i've been waiting years for this book and im stuck between screaming in fear and excitement, with schwab you can never really tell<br /><br /><b>buddy read</b> with the squaf💗, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10502567-jiana" rel="nofollow noopener">🐝</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/36873117-maram" rel="nofollow noopener">👸</a>, &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/61624004-amy" rel="nofollow noopener">🐀</a></span>

<div id="review_3094715758" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3094715758" />
    <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik"><img alt="Nilufer Ozmekik" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559807601p2/53701594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3094715758?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nilufer Ozmekik" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nilufer Ozmekik" href="/user/show/53701594-nilufer-ozmekik">Nilufer Ozmekik</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3094715758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13682358907792545806">OMG! It took toooooooooooo long to finish this book and I wish the third book will come out sooner because I didn’t get my enough intake of Eli and Victor! They didn’t feature at this book as much as I expected. Dammit!<br/><br/>Well, I enjoyed the first one so much. It was one of darkest, bloody nightmares and I seriously fell in love with the writing. The second installment is also dark, vulgar, violent, bloodier, stunning and introducing us toughest villanelles which was the weakest point of the first </span>
  <span id="freeText13682358907792545806" style="display:none">OMG! It took toooooooooooo long to finish this book and I wish the third book will come out sooner because I didn’t get my enough intake of Eli and Victor! They didn’t feature at this book as much as I expected. Dammit!<br /><br />Well, I enjoyed the first one so much. It was one of darkest, bloody nightmares and I seriously fell in love with the writing. The second installment is also dark, vulgar, violent, bloodier, stunning and introducing us toughest villanelles which was the weakest point of the first book not to have enough female characters instead of Sydney. But its longevity slows the pacing and it seems like I have read two additional books at the same time (It could be more than three books. That wasn’t necessary to write only trilogies! If my favorite author writes more than five books with these amazing <br />characters, I will read them without thinking a second!)<br /><br />BUT… yes something is with this one. It’s good but not sooo great! Not my kind of mind blowing, wow my mind keep spinning kind of controversial five starred reading. But I have to admit the author mesmerized us with mind numbing time zone trick. Yes, you got lost in several of them. So this book reminding me of complex mathematical equation. <br /><br />Let’s talk about newbies: Marcella and June. Femme fatale and shapeshifter badass. They are cruel, wild and dangerous. Marcella is breathtakingly beautiful nemesis and don’t forget the mysterious June become a real good sister to Sydney.<br /><br />The complex relationship of Eli (I'm still visualizing him as Michael Fassbender )and Victor (He could be played by James McAvoy and I will enjoy every second of it) salute us again and guess what we read more about Eli’s backstory which makes you scream, pissed off, break your heart into tiny pieces and you get the reason why he chose a path to become a villain. <br /><br />Mostly I enjoyed the parts of my favorite trio from the first book: Victor-Mitch-Sydney: My dangerous modern three musketeers, another version of modern family.<br /><br />This world building, amazing character development and dark themes always fascinate me. I don’t want to wait for the third one so long and I wished it will be released at the end of this year. Well another waiting for Godot situation for me and I became Vladimir again.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13682358907792545806" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2458029568" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2458029568" />
    <a title="☆ Mira ✷" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59512872-mira"><img alt="☆ Mira ✷" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533385624p2/59512872.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2458029568?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Mira ✷" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Mira ✷" href="/user/show/59512872-mira">☆ Mira ✷</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781789090772" href="/book/show/42073914-vengeful">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=twisty-plot-twists">twisty-plot-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=speculative-fiction">speculative-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=schwab-in-the-wild">schwab-in-the-wild</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=6-stars">6-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=favorite-protagonists">favorite-protagonists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=antiheroes">antiheroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=made-me-flip-out">made-me-flip-out</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=mystery-thriller">mystery-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/59512872-mira?shelf=my-idea-of-literary-merit">my-idea-of-literary-merit</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2458029568" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13046121000865805572"><b>#hide yo kids hide yo wife schwab came for us all</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1539121743i/26425407._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>^me meeting Victoria Schwab the day after I finished <i>Vengeful</i> and trying not to be freakishly starstruck. (she said she loved my "Victor Vale is my hero" shirt, which is <b>peak fangirl</b> try and top me. Also, I always thought that she must be the Devil & Co due to how her books screw me over, but she's so sweet and funny, she definitely has no Satanic origins.)<br/><br/>Anyway, after finishing <i>Vengeful</i>, I spent 10 mins searching GIF websites for variations of "</span>
  <span id="freeText13046121000865805572" style="display:none"><b>#hide yo kids hide yo wife schwab came for us all</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1539121743i/26425407._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>^me meeting Victoria Schwab the day after I finished <i>Vengeful</i> and trying not to be freakishly starstruck. (she said she loved my "Victor Vale is my hero" shirt, which is <b>peak fangirl</b> try and top me. Also, I always thought that she must be the Devil &amp; Co due to how her books screw me over, but she's so sweet and funny, she definitely has no Satanic origins.)<br><br>Anyway, after finishing <i>Vengeful</i>, I spent 10 mins searching GIF websites for variations of "death, satan, ghost, hell" to express how I feel about <i>Vengeful</i> only to accept that nothing can do it justice, so that's the Schwab Effect™. <br><br>I mean, I just want to know what grave sin I committed in a past life to deserve that <i>fireball</i> of an ending?! I KNOW there will be a third book—that cliffhangerish hell can't possibly be the last we see of Merit. I teared up in class today, probably looking like I was crying about math, but really I was just thinking about a <i>certain event</i> at the end about which I'll be Emotional for the next century.<br><br>But I also must have been a saint at some point to be born into a world where the Villains duology exists, because, you know, when there's intense pain, the happiness is that much stronger, or something like that. And there's a LOT of enjoyment here. So many BADASS things kept happening that made me grin in delight. Whenever I sat down to read, 100 addictive pages would go by before I knew it. <br><br>Especially during the climax. The climax felt like a roller coaster, except that roller coasters <i>warn</i> you about the potential side effects, and it's socially acceptable to scream at the top of your lungs during them. My heart was beating faster than it does when I think I've finally trapped a spider under a cup, only to lift it and see empty space. And then the ending—WHAT?! That's going on my gravestone.<br><br>I'm in awe of how Victoria draws out tension and develops relationships between characters over months or years that they spend <i>not interacting at all</i>. In AGOS, Kell &amp; Lila didn't even make eye contact until the last 18% of the book, yet their relationship was MY LIFE the ENTIRE time. In <i>Vengeful</i>, this type of dynamic takes place between Victor &amp; Eli; they've been apart for 5 years and don't reunite until the climax, but we get all the feels from their friendship/enmity. <br><br>Speaking of Victor/Eli feels, THOSE <b>ELI EMOTIONS</b> WHAT ON EARTH. I can't believe we got Holland'ed again?! Join my Eli Protection Program 2k18 PLEASE. <br><br>BUT anyway, let's get to the point and talk about <b>Marcella Morgan</b>, the real star of <i>Vengeful</i>. She's the icon of my life, a truly aspirational EO with the power of burning what she touches. Naturally, she uses this power to burn trash ass men down and rise to power. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Marcella wondered how many men she would have to turn to ash before one took her seriously.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Every time I thought she couldn't get more savage, she went and Did That. With the time-skipping format of this series, we learn Marcella's life story, which sets up an amazing character arc. How she views her femininity and draws power from it throughout her life, and how that evolves, is fascinating. <br><br>Which brings me to my next declaration: <i>Vengeful</i> is the feminist antihero story I never knew I needed. It's the most feminist SFF I've EVER read. The juxtaposition of the ways in which Marcella, June, and Sydney are suppressed and how they react to it is incredibly effective. The themes in <i>Vengeful</i> are for you to figure out—Victoria doesn't straight out <i>tell</i> you anything—which made this feminist aspect <b>subtly executed but <i>so</i> powerful. </b><br><br>Back to how I met Victoria Schwab on tour (!), she talked about the feminism in <i>Vengeful</i>, and I diligently memorized what she said. Whereas <i>Vicious</i> is very masculine and focuses on male friendships, toxic masculinity, etc, <i>Vengeful</i> is all about the women and how they reclaim power. Marcella is a mob wife always treated as an object. Sydney, due to her not aging, is frustratingly infantilized by everyone, both by strangers and by those who love her. Then there's June, and... well... Victoria just started enthusiastically talking about how June is a living, breathing, voodoo doll, seeming (righteously) proud of herself for this. ("She's like Mystique from X-Men, except that if she gets hurt, the other person will feel it!")<br><br><b>The flow of power</b> is another main theme, building on what started in <i>Vicious</i> and linking to the aforementioned feminism. I spent 2 hours today just thinking intensely about Victoria's statements in this book about power and how it corrupts. The parallels and contrasts between Marcella &amp; Victor, Marcella &amp; Eli, and Victor &amp; Eli's use of power are SO INTERESTING. My loyal followers probably aren't loyal enough to read 1k words of literary analysis in an innocuous review of a superhero thriller, but the person reading this is welcome to slide into my DMs anytime ;)<br><br>It was also illuminating to think about how Marcella compares to Adelina from The Young Elites. Their narrative arcs are close parallels despite the series being so different.<br><br>&lt;3 so anyway, this too long review is a small sampling of my reactions to <i>Vengeful</i>, the book of my life that makes me want to be the next King Arthur so I can declare it required reading for every high school in the kingdom I rule.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13046121000865805572" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a title="amy ☂︎" class="user" itemprop="url" name="amy ☂︎" href="/user/show/61624004-amy">amy ☂︎</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61624004-amy?shelf=2018">2018</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2547040907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2997028860210868588">this.......................... was everything i wanted, truly.<br/><br/>i don't know how schwab does it but somehow she just manages to wrap her series up so perfectly. i loved every single word in this book, i lived and breathed victor, syd, mitch and even eli, i clutched my heart so many times i lost count. <b>I LOVE THIS BOOK WITH EVERY PART OF MY SOUL I JUST WANT TO SCREAM IT INTO THE WORLD!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>i'm so filled with love and pain, i don't even know how to put <i>any of it</i> into words.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540288782i/26487528._SX540_.jpg' width='350' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/>i feel like </span>
  <span id="freeText2997028860210868588" style="display:none">this.......................... was everything i wanted, truly.<br><br>i don't know how schwab does it but somehow she just manages to wrap her series up so perfectly. i loved every single word in this book, i lived and breathed victor, syd, mitch and even eli, i clutched my heart so many times i lost count. <b>I LOVE THIS BOOK WITH EVERY PART OF MY SOUL I JUST WANT TO SCREAM IT INTO THE WORLD!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br>i'm so filled with love and pain, i don't even know how to put <i>any of it</i> into words.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540288782i/26487528._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>i feel like nothing i'm about to say is going to do this masterpiece of a book justice, but i'm sure as hell going to try anyways.<br><br>let's talk <b>
  <u>CHARACTERS</u>
</b>:<br><br>the characters are always what makes or breaks a book for me, and i have to say, nobody quite does characters like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7168230.V_E__Schwab" title="V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">V.E. Schwab</a>. it's just so much fun to follow these deliciously complex, real, carefully crafted characters along on their journey, and schwab just manages to make you feel for them.<br><br>♦ <b>Victor fucking Vale</b><br><br>first of all, i want victor vale to roundhouse kick me in the face. i just aggressively love him so much, it's borderline insane.<br><br>he doesn't fuck around, and that's what i love about him. he just unapologetically does his thing, with no remorse, no sympathy, no second thoughts. never without a plan A, B or fucking Y. <br><b>i adore him with every inch of my being</b>. if anybody ever outranks kaz brekker for me, it might be victor vale. he is just so unabashedly <b>victor vale</b>, and i would propel myself into the sun for him.<br><br>i wish i could follow him along on his adventures for 1000 more books<br><br>♣ <b>Syd, Mitch, and Dol</b><br><br>i just adore their unwavering love for each other. they still don't know how to show it, so that hasn't changed since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23688792.These_Vicious_Masks__These_Vicious_Masks___1_" title="These Vicious Masks (These Vicious Masks, #1) by Tarun Shanker" rel="nofollow noopener">vicious</a>, but i do feel like their bond grew even stronger. it's so bluntly evident to everyone evolved that they would die for each other, and that's so beautiful to me. every time mitch was a loving grump it made flowers bloom in my chest. <br>i also still think about the fact that he has syd saved as "tiny terror" in his phone sjdksdjhfk i just love them too much what the fuck???<br><br>♥ <b>Marcella</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"How many men would she have to turn to dust before one took her seriously?"</i>
</blockquote><br>i think most of us can #relate<br><br>marcella is a delicious new character that we got in this book. she takes what she wants, doesn't really care about consequences, and wants to see the world burn. i liked her POV, it was very interesting. <br><br>however, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[i feel like her end didn't really do her character justice. all throughout the book she was made up to be this powerful, invincible woman and then she just dies rather quickly and unspectacularly <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>i would've loved to see even more of her.<br><br>♠ <b>Eli Ever</b><br><br>i can't believe schwab actually made me sympathize with him, what kind of sick manipulation bullshit is this<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540290384i/26487611._SX540_.jpg" width="340" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>(mayhaps i don't have too much of a problem with that)<br><br>we get more of eli's backstory in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26856502.Vengeful__Villains___2_" title="Vengeful (Villains, #2) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">vengeful</a>. however, schwab manages to avoid a redemption arc; she doesn't give any type of justification for his errors, simply states "this is why he is how he is" without apologizing him in any way or giving him credit. i love that. <br><br>i definitely learned to appreciate his character more. i might have even carved a small space into my heart for him. eli ever, you sick bastard. i kinda love you.<br><br><br><b>
  <u>PLOT, WRITING, ALL THE GOOD STUFF:</u>
</b><br><br>going into this book, i was utterly terrified, because schwab has too much power over me and she kills me every time i touch a book of hers.<br><br><blockquote>
<u>someone:</u> "what scares you?"<br><u>me, with a horrified expression:</u> "the last book in a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7168230.V_E__Schwab" title="V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">v.e. schwab</a> series"</blockquote><br><br>schwab does everything right in this book. where i struggled with the beginning of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23688792.These_Vicious_Masks__These_Vicious_Masks___1_" title="These Vicious Masks (These Vicious Masks, #1) by Tarun Shanker" rel="nofollow noopener">vicious</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26856502.Vengeful__Villains___2_" title="Vengeful (Villains, #2) by V.E. Schwab" rel="nofollow noopener">vengeful</a> was <b>flawlessly paced</b> from the start. i wasn't bored for one second. at this point i feel like i could've kept reading for another 800 pages. <br><br>her writing is superb, as usual. i don't know how she manages to have the <b>right words at the right places</b>, but she just kinda makes everything look easy. she was born to be a writer, and you can feel it with every word, every sentence, every page. <br><br><b>the whole plot was executed perfectly.</b> the ending was satisfying, but so was the entire build-up. schwab left nothing out, there was nothing more to be desired, she covered everything that wasn't covered in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23688792.These_Vicious_Masks__These_Vicious_Masks___1_" title="These Vicious Masks (These Vicious Masks, #1) by Tarun Shanker" rel="nofollow noopener">vicious</a> and beyond that. <br><br>this book had me at the edge of my seat constantly, even when nothing particularly exciting was happening. it was thrilling in a subliminal way. there was some kind of <i>pull</i> to it that didn't let me go until i was done reading it.<br><br>all in all it was an addicting, enthralling, satisfying experience. i feel both dead inside and weirdly accomplished all at once. and of course incredibly sad that we live in a simulation where we possibly won't get a third book in this series. this is what pain feels like, i guess. <b>but i'm so glad that this book is a part of me now.</b><br><br>hey............ check this series out if you haven't. trust me on this one.<br><br><blockquote>
<i>"His eyes met Victor's, and for a second neither man moved. <b>Run</b>, thought Victor, and he could see the response in Eli's coiled frame.<br><b>Chase me.</b>"</i><br><br>_______<br><br><br><blockquote>
<b>✦ buddy read</b> with the squad: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508-may" rel="nofollow noopener">maymay</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10502567-jiana" rel="nofollow noopener">gianna</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/36873117-maram#comment_form" rel="nofollow noopener">marami</a>
</blockquote>
</blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2414361983" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2414361983" />
    <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65321843-a"><img alt="✨ A ✨ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604503440p2/65321843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2414361983?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨ A ✨ " href="/user/show/65321843-a">✨ A ✨ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/41568127-vengeful">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=five-stars">five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=faves-adult-scifi-and-fantasy">faves-adult-scifi-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=2018-release">2018-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=all-the-stars-in-the-sky">all-the-stars-in-the-sky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2414361983" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13729326473084780727">I finished this book over a week ago and have procrastinated this review because <b>I AM STILL</b> completely <b>S H O O K</b>. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1540068401ra/26477892.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It took a while to put my thoughts together. And I will now attempt to express my love for this book and all these kick-ass characters, who are all so dear to me. <br/><br/><u>
  <b>SPOILERS BELOW</b>
</u><br/><br/>The five year time jump came as a surprise, though not an unwelcome one. Throughout the book there was plenty time jumping and changing of POV, but I managed to keep up and I didn't mind. <br/><br/>After the end of </span>
  <span id="freeText13729326473084780727" style="display:none">I finished this book over a week ago and have procrastinated this review because <b>I AM STILL</b> completely <b>S H O O K</b>. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1540068401ra/26477892.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It took a while to put my thoughts together. And I will now attempt to express my love for this book and all these kick-ass characters, who are all so dear to me. <br><br><u>
  <b>SPOILERS BELOW</b>
</u><br><br>The five year time jump came as a surprise, though not an unwelcome one. Throughout the book there was plenty time jumping and changing of POV, but I managed to keep up and I didn't mind. <br><br>After the end of <i>Vicious</i>, when Sydney resurrects Victor, everything is good for a while. But it soon becomes apparent that there is something very wrong with Victor and his powers. <br>And so begins the search for a solution: an EO healer. But with each dead-end their desperation increases. <br><br><b>
  <i>Mitch and Sydney shouldn’t have come at all, but Victor had long given up trying to dissuade them. Attachment was a vexing thing, as pernicious as weeds.</i>
</b><br><br>I loved Victor even more in <i>Vengeful</i>. I felt his hopelessness and I was praying for him to find a remedy. He cares so much for Sydney and Mitch my hearts cracks. <br><br><b>
  <i>...couldn’t bear the look on Sydney’s face. Or Mitch’s.<br>He could leave.<br>Should leave.<br>Distance wouldn’t save him, but it might protect them.</i>
</b><br><br>Mitch ( who is my favourite Schwab character) is Sydney and Victor's anchor in <i>Vengeful</i>. He made each place they were staying in into a home. He worries about both of them. Victor goes around looking for healer EO's and murdering people. And Sydney is resurrecting dead animals in her room. But Mitch? Oh he's making everyone hot cocoa and cooking. I. FUCKIN’. LOVE. HIM. <br><br><br>Sydney finds out that Victor killed Serena. She feels betrayed, but she also realises that Serena was dangerous. AND YET she still starts to strengthen her powers in order to bring Serena back! I get that she misses her though. But that bitch was crazy. <b>Leave her <u>dead</u> I say!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Once upon a time, Victor had promised Sydney that he wouldn’t let anyone hurt her—that he would always hurt them first.<br>He’d broken that promise.</i>
</b><br><br>I really felt for Sydney. She's a teenager stuck in a kids body. So she has no one her age to talk to, and she has <b>two overprotective daddies.</b> I don't blame her for befriending June. She needed someone other than Mitch and Victor, someone else she could vent to. <br><br>I know a lot of people wish that Schwab would have expanded a bit more on June's past. Nope, not me. I didn't like her from the get-go. What happened to her was terrible. But she was still a wacko. <br><br><br>I was actually looking forward to Dominic playing a bigger role in this book. He did and I loved reading his chapters. But then he had to go and get himself killed. <br><b>AND OH MY WORD THE T E A R S</b><br><br><br>Marcella, I thought, was so fun to read about. She's a woman on a mission. And no one will stand in her way. She was just <b>so bad-ass.</b> And I was torn between cheering for her and being like: <i>woman chill now!</i> <br><br><b>
  <i>“Never underestimate an angry woman.”<br>“Never underestimate a woman,”</i>
</b><br><br><br>Eli stole the show for me. I was hoping that we would get to read about his past. You know what they say: <i>be careful what you wish for.</i> Eli's chapters B R O K E M E. <br><br>THE TEARS WOULD NOT STOP FLOWING. And as if his past wasn't torture enough, we jump to the present <b>WHERE HE IS BEING DISSECTED LIKE A FUCKIN’ RAT.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443939594ra/16432635.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Are you trying to kill us V.E Schwab? Because it sure felt like it. <br>But then relief comes when Stell gets him to help on cases instead. <br><br><b>
  <i>Eli had never known there were so many kinds of happiness, let alone so many ways to express it.</i>
</b><br><br>When he was in captivity there was a second I thought maybe he'd turned a new leaf. Maybe he won't want to murder Victor anymore. He'll get out of prison and he can join their family!<br><br>(I've been told I have a wild imagination.) Alas, my dreams were not meant to be. My poor Eli is deceased. It's taken me over a week to get over it. <br><br><br>I am <b>
  <i>REALLY HOPING</i>
</b> for a continuation. I don't mind open-endings, but seriously we NEEEED more. And if there's another book, I'd really love to know more about Victor's childhood and past. I think there's still so much about his character that everyone would love to know more about.<br>____<br><s>I am feeling so many emotions right now. This was <b>AMAZING</b>. <u>Thank you to everyone on Goodreads for hyping VE Schwab.</u> Her work is gold of a discovery for me. I'm so glad I read this series. <b>Review to come</b></s><br>____<br><b>30, Sept 2018</b><br><b>
  <u>Pre-read Rambles</u>
</b><br>My expectations are very high. <b>Life will be hard</b> if this isn't all that I hope it will be. Good vibes this way pleeease XD</span>
  <a data-text-id="13729326473084780727" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2563158043" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2563158043" />
    <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey"><img alt="Chelsea Humphrey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585613513p2/47207032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2563158043?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea Humphrey" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey">Chelsea Humphrey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780765387523" href="/book/show/37534835-vengeful">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Chelsea by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1695365-victoria-schwab">Victoria Schwab</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47207032-chelsea-humphrey?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2563158043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16254323954373186139"><i>*Sigh*</i> This was great. Such a satisfying end to a wholly enjoyable duology. <s>Or is it?</s> JK, but I'm always hopeful that authors will return to my favorite worlds to continue stories on, even if it be through supporting character's stories. Marcella and June were exciting additions to the cast, and my mind is blown by how intricately the timelines were weaved together to keep our attention grasped. Highly recommend these books to folks who enjoy deep character studies of characters that are beyond </span>
  <span id="freeText16254323954373186139" style="display:none"><i>*Sigh*</i> This was great. Such a satisfying end to a wholly enjoyable duology. <s>Or is it?</s> JK, but I'm always hopeful that authors will return to my favorite worlds to continue stories on, even if it be through supporting character's stories. Marcella and June were exciting additions to the cast, and my mind is blown by how intricately the timelines were weaved together to keep our attention grasped. Highly recommend these books to folks who enjoy deep character studies of characters that are beyond the surface definition of evil. </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ORuTcbX1A0Iw5BSX/YPUx4My1yq+v2IXfV/vn+zFs41AV6REyZpPeePayv77pgqIFcOp3wxKQ8mnGhNR0j4lHw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ak6XcUS+R4Eyq2eBBbHgi7bMWyo8knJtRSpZ2Cobaat7AqBEONELuuGVuegDlD7EID0l345nU7Ofb6UWFOD/OQ==')})
  }
